
campaignTrail_temp.cyoa = true;

function getQuestionNumberFromPk(pk) {
    return campaignTrail_temp.questions_json.map(q=>q.pk).indexOf(pk)-1;
}

cyoAdventure = function (a) {
    ans = campaignTrail_temp.player_answers[campaignTrail_temp.player_answers.length-1];

    if (ans == 42343) {
        campaignTrail_temp.question_number = getQuestionNumberFromPk(42344);
    }
    else if (ans == 42918) {
        campaignTrail_temp.question_number = getQuestionNumberFromPk(42973);
    }
    else if (ans == 42922) {
        campaignTrail_temp.question_number = getQuestionNumberFromPk(42973);
    }
    else if (ans == 42925) {
        campaignTrail_temp.question_number = getQuestionNumberFromPk(42973);
    }
    else if (ans == 42901) {
        campaignTrail_temp.question_number = getQuestionNumberFromPk(42937);
    }
    else {
        return false;
    }
}

    function setImage(url) {
        if(url == '' || url == null) return;
        let interval = setInterval(function () {
            img = document.getElementsByClassName("person_image")[0];
            if (img != null) {
                img.src = url;
                clearInterval(interval);
            }
        }, 50);
    }

 to { opacity: 1; }

 </style>
</head>
<body>
 <div class="fade-in">
 <div class="harris-text">
 My fellow Americans,
 <br><br>
 I did not come here tonight expecting to give this speech. But here I stand — as your President-elect.
 <br><br>
 This was not a victory won on a campaign stage. This was not a moment chosen by the people in the way we are used to. This was a moment <span class="harris-tip">
 forged by crisis
 <span class="harris-tooltip-box">
 The courts ruled. The Constitution held. But the nation was shaken.
 </span>
 </span>, and tempered by uncertainty.
 <br><br>
 Let me say it plainly: the outcome of this election was <span class="harris-tip">
 irregular
 <span class="harris-tooltip-box">
 The Electoral College failed to coalesce. The House decided in my favor. That truth must be acknowledged.
 </span>
 </span>. And yet, the law is the law. The Constitution speaks — and it has spoken now through the House of Representatives.
 <br><br>
 I will not pretend that this was the way I envisioned ascending to this office. But neither will I shy away from the responsibility now placed upon me. I take this solemn duty not in celebration, but in <span class="harris-tip">
 reverence
 <span class="harris-tooltip-box">
 To govern after such a fracture is not a triumph — it is a charge to heal.
 </span>
 </span>.
 <br><br>
 To those who voted for the other ticket — who feel robbed, stunned, or angry — I hear you. I do not stand above you. I stand among you, and I will work every day to rebuild the trust this outcome has shaken.
 <br><br>
 To those who fought for me, who organized, who believed even in the darkest hours — I offer you not joy, but <span class="harris-tip">
 purpose
 <span class="harris-tooltip-box">
 There is work ahead — harder than any campaign. Now we must govern.
 </span>
 </span>. This presidency does not begin in celebration. It begins in repair.
 <br><br>
 But let me tell you something I know: **America is not broken beyond repair.** We are bruised. We are bitter. We are tired. But we are not finished.
 <br><br>
 I am ready to serve. I am ready to listen. And I am ready to prove that even in strange and stormy times, the rule of law — and the will to lead with dignity — can still guide us home.
 <br><br>
 Thank you. May God bless you. And may God bless the United States of America.

Like the tide washing over ash, we rise with clarity, mercy, and resolve. We know what must come next.</p>

 <p>We will rebuild—not only what was broken in recent years, but what was quietly crumbling long before. The Voting Rights Act will live again. Gerrymanders will fall. Democracy won’t be something you *fight* to reach—it will be the ground beneath your feet. Truth commissions, reform, and yes—healing. Not because we forget what came before, but because we’ve *survived* it. To those who once cheered chaos: *You are not our enemy*. You are our family, and your children deserve better than the anger you were handed.</p>

 <p>Tonight, I remember a quiet moment before stepping on stage—<span class="harris-tip">alone<span class="harris-tooltip-box">Her breath caught, thinking: *Will they ever believe this actually happened?*</span></span>. Then I heard you—a nation exhaling after holding its breath too long. This was never about a campaign. It was a covenant—between past and future, pain and promise. We’ve done what generations said was impossible. Now we must live lives worthy of that impossibility—with justice, decency, and love as our strategy—not our weakness.</p>

 <p>Tonight, the storm has passed. The sky is still. The republic endures.</p>

</div>
